    SCCC notched up profit growth of 47% y‐y in 4QFY15 chiefly boosted by higher other income andSG&A; expense savings. In this period, quarterly revenue slipped 2% y‐y as revenue from cement salesedged up a meager 1% y‐y driven by a modest pickup in domestic demand and higher export saleswhile revenue from concrete sales plunged 9% y‐y as a result of a persistent slowdown in residentialconstruction activity and due to the fact that the government’s new infrastructure projects were inthe bidding process. Despite revenue drop, well managed energy costs and SG&A; expense savingscoupled with other exceptional income of more than Bt100mn enabled SCCC to deliver a 36% y‐y risein 4QFY15 profit before exceptional items. As the results in this period included a FX gain of Bt94mn,up substantially from Bt13mn in the same year‐ago period, quarterly net profit therefore came in atBt958mn, up 47% y‐y. For the whole of FY15, net profit however dropped 10% y‐y to Bt4,579mn.Following results announcement, SCCC declared a 2HFY15 dividend of Bt7/share. The stock will tradeex‐dividend (XD) on Apr 18, 2016.   
    Profit set to return to slight growth in FY16 helped by revival in demand amid rising competitionfrom TPIPL’s new supply   
    Cement demand in Thailand is expected to grow by 3%‐5% this year. In our view, the prospect of apickup in public construction activity would act as a key catalyst for growth in the second half ofthe year as construction for new projects which have been put up for bids since 4QFY15 is slated toget off the ground in 2HFY16. However, the startup of TPIPL’s fourth cement plant with an annualproduction capacity of 4mn tons would push the country’s domestic cement capacity higher to60mn tons from 56mn tons. At a normal operating rate of 85%, supply would be around 51mntons while demand is estimated at 40mn tons, leaving the country with a supply surplus of 11mntons. Earlier TPIPL’s new supply was destined for exports but we are concerned that it may changeits mind to turn to domestic market as domestic selling prices are higher than export selling prices.If so, competition is set to rise as SCCC and TPIPL have no overseas distribution channels like SCC.Higher competition would also make it difficult to raise selling prices this year but a likely revival indemand should take some pressure off the competition. Our forecast assumes (i) SCCC will achieveFY16 sales growth of 4% on expectations that it will retain its share in the domestic cementmarket, (ii) gross profit margin will hold steady as the negative impact of falling selling prices wouldbe offset by a drop in energy costs along with declining oil prices and (iii) SG&A; expenses will driftlower thanks to its efforts to cut operating expenses. On this basis, we expect SCCC to return toslight profit growth of 6% this year after a 10% contraction last year.   
    ‘BUY’ rating with Bt340/share target price   
    Valuation‐wise, SCCC looks too undervalued to pass up at 13x FY16 P/E, a big discount to its historicalmean of 16x despite the prospect of a return to profit growth of 6% in FY16 after a 10% contractionin FY15 and with an estimated dividend yield of between 5%‐6%. We reiterate a ‘BUY’ call on SCCCshares with a Bt340/share target price in view of compelling valuation and earnings recovery story.

    周小川谈人民币汇率机制改革:在世界经济和全球贸易增速放缓、国际金融市场波动加剧的背景下,现在中国对全球GDP增长的贡献率在25%左右,是比较接近常态的,这不是什么硬着陆。中国2009年、2010年对全球GDP增长的贡献率超过50%,是特殊时期的情况,50%不能当标准用,也是不可持续的。人民币汇率对一篮子货币保持了基本稳定,还有所升值,不存在持续贬值的基础。对汇率改革要有耐心,方向是更加依靠市场力量决定价格,实现更有灵活性的汇率。

SINA	纺织服装行业2015年业绩前瞻:四季度终端消费不振,公司主业...	长江证券股份有限公司	雷玉	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3125679/index.phtml	报告要点   
    行业轨迹:成本下行利好纺织制造,服装消费步入中速增长阶段   
    回顾2015年,以棉花为主的原材料价格下行叠加人民币贬值,成本下行利好纺织制造业。虽然行业整体营收规模进一步下滑、但整体营利能力逐步改善,在历经三年多的调整后出口规模依然延续弱势但结构逐步调整、趋势向上的拐点基本确立。居民服装家纺产品消费整体增速下移、增势趋缓,服饰类消费步入中速增长阶段。行业整体营收和利润增速下行趋势进一步延续,但营利能力逐步改善,在新常态的背景下,GDP增速和居民收入增速放缓以及服装家纺消费习惯逐步成熟,参照美、日历史同期消费情况,我们认为我国的服饰类消费步入中速增长阶段。   
    业绩前瞻:逾半数纺服企业业绩预增,棉纺企业表现亮眼   
    我们预计全年纺织服装板块整体业绩有望实现15%左右的增长。其中,纺织制造板块全年整体业绩有望超过20%的增长、棉纺企业业绩表现尤为亮眼,服装家纺板块有望实现正增长、板块内公司业绩分化显著。根据目前已披露的56家(共82家)纺织服装行业上市公司业绩快报和业绩预告,上述公司2015年合计实现净利润为59.1~75.1亿元,相同口径下较去年增长5.1~33.7%。剔除非主营业务导致的增长后,业绩预增公司共15家(包括4家纺织制造类企业和11家服装家纺类企业),此外有4家公司全年实现扭亏。   
    重点关注业绩稳增长、低估值且具备外延扩张空间的价值型个股   
    2016年,预计纺织服装行业投资并购势头将进一步延续,企业布局新兴领域、有望形成新的利润增长点。继续持续看好纺织服装行业2016年的发展,重点关注业绩稳增长、低估值且具备外延扩张空间的价值型个股。推荐:   
    (1)立足女性和儿童群体,处于高景气度的细分子行业,具备基本面支撑的汇洁股份、朗姿股份和森马服饰,以及以资金博弈为主的高弹性标的乔治白和大杨创世;

SINA	TMT行业:猴年流量猴赛雷,流量经营即起飞	华安证券股份有限公司	华安证券研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3125665/index.phtml	事件:   
    根据工信部最新公布的数据:今年春节假期7天内,手机用户共消费了12780.3万G移动互联网流量,是2015年的2.6倍。平均每个用户使用135.7M,比平日流量高出50%。而全国移动短信发送量累计达到139.6亿条,仅为2015年的三分之二;移动电话去话通话时长累计完成733.9亿分钟,同比下降4.5%。   
    政策保障、需求驱动、技术升级,构建流量经营生态圈   
    “提速降费,流量不清零”——OTT之幸,运营商之殇。克强总理在国务院会议中指出电信企业要实施宽带免费提速,降低资费水平,流量不清零、流量转赠等服务。政策的颁布为OTT厂商来来利好,有助于减少用户手机上网时对于流量资费的担心,相应也会在一定程度上增加上网行为和流量使用。几家欢乐几家愁,随着运营商年底含泪庆祝降费指标的完成,运营商业绩则是雪上加霜,单单“次月流量不清零”一项,预计行业减收240亿,此举也会促进运营商“革自己的命”向流量经营转型。   
    “66岁的妈妈也开始加装流量包”——用户群体扩大,消费习惯养成。根据cnnic最新发布的报告,截至2015年12月我国手机网民规模达6.2亿,使用手机上网的人群占比达90.1%。过去移动上网用户主要以70后-90后为主要群体,现在随着移动互联网应用和智能终端的普及,10岁以下低龄群体和40岁以上中高龄群体占比均有所提升且持续向两端渗透。经过十几年的发展,移动用户月户均流量达到389.3M,同比增长89.9%,内容涉及的衣食住行已成过去式,医疗、理财等新形式出现大幅提升。作为产业链上游的最终用户,用户群体的扩大和消费习惯的养成为流量经营打下良好基础。   
    “3G、4G已快用烦,5G还会远吗”——技术更新迭代,应用升级加快。通信行业呈现出一定的周期性,通常每5年左右就会进行一次技术升级。自从2013年底发放LTE牌照,到目前4G用户已基本赶超3G,而5G将在2018-2020年开始试商用和商用。在理想情况下如果从网上下载一部1GB的高清视频,3G可能需要几十分钟,4G可能需要十几分钟,而5G则只要几秒钟。上网速率加快势必会带来诸如高清视频,VR等大型高流量应用的推广,有助于构建流量经营生态圈,否则几十米宽的高速公路已经修好,在上面只骑自行车岂不浪费?q前向流量经营模式创新,后向流量经营挖掘潜力前向流量经营商务模式推陈出新。前向流量经营是指用户按照运营商的要求订购流量套餐包并向运营商付费的方式,也是目前的主流方式。   
    随着移动互联网和用户需求的发展,在传统套餐包、流量包的基础上,还出现了流量币、流量券、流量银行等多种可交易的创新商业模式。运营商阵营已经纷纷出招,如中国电信“流量宝”、中国移动“爱流量”,中国联通“流量商店”;第三方厂商阵营也有如魔品科技“麦流量”,腾畅科技“流米”等。这些应用不仅可以实现流量订购,也可以通过做任务等方式获取流量、转赠流通,注入了一些娱乐和社交等互联网属性,实现了前向流量经营模式的创新。虽然这些应用目前占比较小,但这些新生的事物在一定程度上为乏力的前向流量经营带来了一丝曙光,助力传统方式的变革。   
    投资建议

SINA	海外市场点评:美国非农就业可能会快速滑落	中泰证券股份有限公司	刘启元	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3125647/index.phtml	事件:昨日美国公布重要的非农就业数据,美股跌了,但美元大涨,同时时薪同比增长,失业率下降,市场反应看似有些矛盾。那么非农数据到底好不好呢?   
    美国就业数据可能就此开始急剧滑落   
    失业率是众所周知的滞后数据,它的下降基本可以忽略不计,那么时薪同比增长是就业好转的证据吗?从已有的2007年以来的数据来看,“次贷危机”中时薪同比增速是从2008年12月份开始剧烈下滑,而工业产出下滑从2007年底就已经开始,到2009年5月份美国经济就已经见底了,因此时薪同比也是一个非常显著的滞后指标,而且其短期的波动性也很大,不足以成为判断就业是否好转的指标。   
    那么回头看新增非农就业数据,尽管它短期的波动性也很高,但对经济增长来说是一个非常好的同比甚至略微领先的指标,而且其波动性也不足以影响其趋势,平滑过的数据具有很强的周期性和波动性,因此是非常重要的指标(ADP就业可以看作是平滑过的非农就业数据,因此也是非常重要的替代指标)。非农就业每一次的下滑都值得重视,尤其是在工业产出和GDP增速已经出现连续两个季度的下滑之后,非农就业数据的初始下滑可能意味着就业新增数据就此开始滑落。   
    因为前几个月的非农就业数据是非常异常的,而其强劲增长的背后有两个驱动因素:一,暖冬促使建筑行业就业异常增加;二,包含政府就业的教育与保健行业就业非常强劲。不过目前这两个因素都已经发生改变:一,美国长期利率攀升已经使房地产市场复苏遭遇疲态,建筑活动也显著放缓;二,政府就业开始减少,其他低端服务业就业也开始减少,因此我们可以预计新增非农就业快速下滑的时间点可能已经到来。历史上来看,新增非农就业下滑到零就意味着美国经济真正遭遇红灯,根据我们的观察,这一时点距离现在并不会太远。	0.132578951795	中国石油 0.00099397875101 中国铝业 0.000986154323996 光线传媒 0.000959144869311 中国中车 0.000928490133855 动力源 0.000895511319462	增长	下降 下滑 减少	传媒 0.878688573837 医药生物 0.0414503961802 化工 0.0176318325102 轻工制造 0.0161371808499 有色金属 0.0143229868263	20160218	10:35

    Asset Quality – UOB has S$21bn exposure to commodity loan book, of that S$12bn isrelated to Oil & Gas which is the deemed to contain the highest risks. The management sees20% of the S$12bn (S$2.4bn) most vulnerable but only under extreme assumptions like oilprices remaining at current levels of US$25 to US$30 per barrel beyond a year. Besides, theS$2.4bn exposure is only 1.1% of loan books and it would take more than a year ofextremely low oil price to decisively impair the US$2.4bn completely. By that same period,UOB would have a full year’s earnings to offset this loss. So it is in the management’sopinion that the current market conditions may be detrimental to income but not to thebalance sheet. The management does not view the S$21bn exposure to Greater China asrisky because they do not see China going into a hard landing situation. 50% of the S$21bnexposure is to China’s top 5 banks and the other 50% non-bank exposure is to top-tier SOEs,large local corporates and foreign investment enterprise. Management also does not see thevolatile RMB moves to impact the balance sheet negatively too.   
    Outlook – Amidst the challenging environment, management would continue to focus onliability management to optimize funding costs and improve net interest margins. Loan toDeposit Ratio increased from 83.8% in FY14 to 84.7% in FY15 because of lower fixeddeposits. And at the same time Current Accounts and Savings Accounts (CASA) increased,reflecting management’s effort to ramp up funding from this segment. CASAs generally bearlower costs and are often stickier but take up a much smaller composition in the depositmix. To boost the funding mix, UOB would be able to leverage on its brand to tap the marketby issuing covered bonds which can be priced competitively under current marketconditions.
SINA	2015年第四季度货币政策报告点评:做好供给侧结构性改革中的...	国信证券股份有限公司	董德志	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3125627/index.phtml	2015年第四季度货币政策报告点评   
    2月6日午间,央行发布了2015年四季度货币政策执行报告。整体来看,2016年货币政策思路的变化主要是做好供给侧结构性改革中的总需求管理。另外,文中也提到,在开放宏观格局下,货币政策面临着汇率“硬约束”以及资产价格国际间“强对比”地约束。   
    一、相比三季度,四季度货政报告对国内外经济的看法整体不变,认为国内经济增速平稳,通胀低位运行。   
    与三季度相比,此次货政报告对国内外经济的看法整体不变。指出在错综复杂的全球经济环境下,中国经济总体保持了中高速增长。另外,物价涨幅在结构调整过程中保持相对较低水平的概率较大。   
    对经济的描述:2015年中国经济运行总体平稳,结构调整积极推进。   
    对国外经济的判断:当前世界经济仍处于深度调整期,全球价值链再造和贸易投资格局在发生变化,主要经济体货币政策进一步分化,地缘政治更趋复杂,不确定、不稳定因素依然较多(三季度表述为:当前世界经济总体仍较为疲弱且呈分化态势,不确定因素较多)。   
    对国内通胀形势的描述:物价涨幅较低、相对稳定,并继续呈现结构化特征(三季度表述为:物价涨幅较低、相对稳定,并呈现结构化特征)。   
    对未来通胀形势判断:物价涨幅保持相对较低水平的概率较大(三季度表述为:物价涨幅低水平运行的概率较大)。   
    二、下一阶段货币政策思路的变化点:做好供给侧结构性改革中的总需求管理,对冲经济下行压力与三季度报告相比,在下一阶段货币政策思路中,新增了“做好供给侧结构性改革中的总需求管理”。同时,专栏6《供给侧结构性改革与总需求管理》里提到,“供给侧结构性改革短期可能会加大经济下行压力,需要做好相应的总需求管理,保持经济运行在合理区间”。   
    也即是说,在中央经济工作会议强调了供给侧结构性改革后,2016年央行的主要重点是做好相应的总需求管理。而总需求管理除了刺激需求、加大基建和房地产投资外,还要依靠供给改革。   
    三、其它亮点:1、在总结2015年时提到,“更加注重稳定短端利率”、“引导货币市场利率平稳下行,并采取有效措施降低货币市场利率波动,优化利率期限结构”。   
    点评:这与我国货币政策加强价格型调控,完善传导机制相符。   
    2、在《专栏5准备金率、流动性与央行资产负债表》中提到,在开放宏观格局下,货币政策面临着汇率“硬约束”以及资产价格国际间“强对比”地约束。本国货币政策过于宽松容易导致本币贬值压力。   
    点评:这解释了近期外储下降较快,但央行迟迟未降准的原因——汇率制约。   
    3、文中提到“化解金融风险”、加强“……民间融资及非法集资、跨境资金流动等领域的风险监测分析”、“依法处置信用违约风险”、“坚决遏制非法集资蔓延势头”等点评:四季度报告对金融风险的涉及多于之前4、提到“2015年末CFETS人民币汇率指数为100.94,人民币对一篮子货币保持了基本稳定”点评:人民币汇率观察视角由“双边汇率”向“篮子货币汇率”转变四、数据方面,执行上浮利率的贷款占比迅速下降,就业率总体平稳。   
    1、贷款利率方面,12月份,非金融企业及其他部门贷款加权平均利率为5.27%,比9月份下降43BP。细项来看,一般贷款利率继续下降37BP,票据融资加权利率下降96BP,个人住房贷款利率继续下降32BP,票据融资利率重回下降通道。从利率浮动情况来看,四季度末执行下浮利率的贷款占比明显提升,执行上浮利率的占比迅速下降。   
    总的来看,虽然2015年10月存款利率上限完全放开,但是这对贷款利率的传导非常有限,四季度信贷供需格局进一步宽松。

<Ignored> SINA	China Oil &Gas;:CNPC,First decl...	摩根大通证券(亚太)有限公司	摩根大通(亚太)研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3125625/index.phtml	The China National Petroleum Corp. (CNPC) published its annual Oil &Gas; Industry Development Report (2015). The China equivalent of BP’sglobal energy statistical review has been widely quoted by the industry andwe believe some of their forecasts and data points would be interesting toyour investment research. We highlight the key bullets below.   
    First decline in China's energy usage in 30 years. According to CNPCestimates, China’s energy consumption fell 1.1% to 4.2 bn tons of standard coalequivalents in 2015, the first contraction in 30 years, and that’s mainly drivenby the country’s economic slowdown and shift in growth drivers. Use of coal(64% of total energy mix in 2015) dropped 3.8%, apparent oil consumption rose4.8% while natural gas usage gained 3.8% and non-fossil fuel rose 8.9%.   
    Policy outlook for next five years. CNPC identified the following as the keypolicy changes in China's oil and gas sector through 2020: (1) allowing morenon-state refineries to import crude oil; (2) separating pipeline assets fromexisting operators and forming several specialized companies; (3) moreadjustment to oil & gas pricing towards a market-based mechanism; (4)allowing more E&P; competition from non SOEs; and (5) restructuring serviceorientedsubsidiaries under the major oil & gas groups with a target of IPO.   
    Slower oil products demand growth. CNPC forecasts average 8% oil productssurplus in China this year and a 31% expansion in net products exports fromChina in 2016 (85% in diesel net exports), highlighting teapot refineries as amajor risk. That confirms our key trip takeaways from the China TeapotRefinery Tour in end Jan (see note). CNPC see challenges to the sustainabilityof current high levels in refinery GRM. Separately, the report also unveilsChina’s total crude stockpile capacity at 495mn bbls (180mn bbls SPR and315mn bbls commercial).   
    CNPC sees rebound in China's gas demand in 2016. CNPC sees a rebound inChina’s gas demand to 7.3% in 2016 (3.7% in 2015), mainly driven by lowerprices and stricter environmental policies. The report sees high single digitgrowth in 2016 gas consumption by city-gas and power-gen users (double digitsin 2015) and low to mid-single digit increase in industrial/chemicals (declines in2015). Domestic gas production may increase 5.5% (3.5% in 2015) whileimports may rise 10.6% due to committed volumes, according to CNPCforecasts.
SINA	中国银行:应对长期信贷周期尚有缓冲空间;结构性问题有待解决	高盛高华证券有限责任公司	李南,吴双	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3125608/index.phtml	潜在不良率有多高?   
    我们预计,受企业盈利(尤其是上游领域)走弱的影响,信贷周期将持续至第五个年头。我们对于工业企业EBIT利息保障倍数的初步分析显示整体潜在不良率约为9%,而2015年底银行业公布的不良率/关注类贷款率分别为1.7%/3.8%。截至2015年前9个月,上市银行的新增不良贷款生成率为1.35%。   
    准信贷资产的总规模多大?   
    我们估算,存在于买入返售/投资项以及表外理财产品的非标信贷资产的规模约为人民币16万亿元。前者(涵盖信托受益权)规模相当于银行总资产的8%,但高度集中于股份制银行和城商行。五大行在这一领域的敞口有限。   
    存在怎样的盈利/资本金缓冲?   
    我们估算,在满足最低资本充足率要求的前提下,商业银行整体可吸收至多11%的不良资产率。银行仍有能力逐步吸收坏账损失;假设中国银行业拨备前营业利润/贷款利润率为3-4%,那么基于当前约为130个基点的信贷成本率,预计银行业需要5-6年时间来消化潜在的不良贷款。   
    监管部门是否会放松150%的拨备覆盖率要求?   
    由于不良贷款快速增长,2015年底全系统的不良贷款拨备覆盖率从一年前的233%降至181%。我们认为银监会可能在今年放松拨备要求,原因在于:1)逆周期的监管框架以及2)大型银行面临盈利压力。这样的举措有利于银行的短期盈利/每股股息。不过,银行的中期盈利前景依然面临挑战,因为拨备可能不足以覆盖约9%的潜在不良率。我们在压力测试中假设银行需要将不良贷款拨备覆盖率保持在65-75%,富余的拨备金可吸收3-4%的不良资产率。   
    主要结构性问题有哪些?   
    1)自2008年以来杠杆率快速上升,尤其是在公司企业领域,2)产能过剩问题随之出现,3)市场清出进程缓慢,不良贷款损失确认迟缓,以及4)有迹象显示银行正加大零售贷款发放,这将促进经济的再平衡。虽然我们相信中国银行业能应对这一充满挑战的运营环境,但是在不良贷款问题全面明朗化且解决方案到位之前,银行股难以出现显著的估值重估。	0.678807285572	华夏银行 0.00119369207322 北京银行 0.00101114995127 国新能源 0.000926937580371 中国中车 0.000885916966319 星期六 0.000885728802622	上升	走弱 难以	商业贸易 0.205980882049 医药生物 0.148881956935 纺织服装 0.140305563807 电气设备 0.0584913045168 计算机 0.0451027005911	20160218	10:35

    公司公告与冯永森签订了《股权转让与增资扩股协议》,由公司收购冯永森先生持有的湖州华特钢管70%的股权;股权转让后再由公司与冯永森各自对华特钢管进行增资。   
    评论   
    收购华特钢管70%股权。本次公司将以自有资金540万元收购自然人股东冯永森先生持有的华特钢管出资额1050万元的70%股权。股权转让完成后,公司与冯永森对华特钢管各自增加投资(公司增资1118万元,冯永森增资476万元)。同时,根据三年业绩承诺,2016-2018年华特钢管扣非后归属母公司净利润不低于150万元、280万元、450万元。若未达到,差额部分由冯永森会通过将其股权以1元/股的价格补偿给久立特材或以现金方式补偿给华特钢管。截至2015年10月31日,华特钢管总资产6846万元,净资产为-458万元,营业收入为5441万元,扣非净利润为-378万元。   
    整合资源,拓展新的下游市场。公司此次收购的华特钢管专业从事工业用不锈钢无缝,现有无缝管产能3000吨,产品主要应用于冷冻装备及空气化工行业等行业。此次收购,一方面将整合加快过剩产能出清,提升行业集中度;另一方面,将在产品、客户等方面与华特钢管形成互补。华特钢管重点服务于批量小、品种规格杂,且着重于空气化工等小众市场,与公司目前所处下游均为国家大型项目、规模化服务形成有效互补。此次并购整合将加快公司在小众领域市场的新品开发和市场份额提升。   
    核电产业链核心标的,继续看好中长期前景。公司作为国内核电用管制造领域的领跑者,除已有的690U型管、外套管、C形传热管等拳头产品外,持续加码核电/军工业务并取得新突破。根据公司在互动平台上表示,目前已有核电及军工方面的在手订单。我们认为,公司是高端特钢的典型代表,核电用管产品在国内核电各代技术路线上均有所布局且技术实力领先,有望充分享受核电盛宴以及军工大发展。虽短期业绩受油气下游影响较大,但我们依然看好公司中长期发展前景。   
    投资建议

    The PBOC released monthly credit data showing a sharp increase in Januaryloan growth. Interestingly, the aggressive expansion comes a day after theCBRC’s quarterly disclosures on commercial banks’ balance sheets showedyet another quarter of asset quality deterioration.   
    Impact   
    System loans expanded by 2.5% MoM / 14.1% YoY. RMB loans jumped+3.3% MoM / +16.0% YoY in Jan, a sharp acceleration from the +0.8% MoM /+14.6% YoY pace in Dec 2015. RMB retail loans grew 2.2% MoM / 17% YoY,with the bulk attributable to MLT loans (largely mortgages). But MLT corporateRMB loans (+3.1% MoM / 46%YoY) were the biggest single growth driver.   
    Total deposits expanded by 1.6% MoM / 12.3% YoY. RMB deposit growthalso recovered from flat Dec performance to post a more sedate growth paceof 1.5% MoM / 12.3% YOY in Jan. This is the first meaningful YoY comp sincethe PBOC widened its definition of deposits in Jan 2015, creating the sharpshifts in the deposit growth and LDR charts at left.   
    LDR ticks higher yet again. The redefinition of deposits caused a 331bpdecline in the system LDR a year ago, but the LDR trend has continuedpersistently higher, especially since June 2015. Under the new definition, thesystem LDR has reached 71.7% with RMB LDR at 70.0%. While that appearsto indicate a high level of bank balance-sheet liquidity, it is crucial to be awarethat only around half of China banks’ IEAs are classified as “loans”.   
    Credit quality continues to worsen. A single month is not a trend andChinese New Year creates a lot of distortion in Jan-Feb economic data. But asustained rapid pace of corporate loan growth could lead to further pain later,in our view, as outlined by yesterday’s CBRC asset quality data.

Sales in February will likely soften on a Y/Y basis with the effect of anearlier CNY this year. However, as it normally takes 8-10 weeks for sales to peakafter policy easing announcement, we believe March will see a very strong pick-upin sales with a potential 15-20% Y/Y growth. We think the positive sentimentbrought by the new policy could last till April, and there might be even more easingannouncements by then. Some other potential easing measures include: (1) HPFeasing, (2) stimuli to secondary market and (3) further lowering of mortgage rate.   
    HKMA will take more time to consider relaxing cooling measures: NormanChan, Chief Executive of the HK Monetary Authority (HKMA), made a statementduring his appearance at the Legislative Council yesterday that HKMA will takemore time to confirm whether the property market has already entered the downcycle. If such is confirmed, HKMA may relax the existing property market coolingmeasures, including loosening on the LTV for residential mortgages. He mentionedthat transaction volumes and home prices have dropped initially but rebounded 6-12months after the implementation of new cooling measures in the past, therefore moretime is needed to evaluate the appropriate window to relax the property coolingmeasures. Also, he reiterated that the current new mortgages in Hong Kong areextended on a 50% LTV on average which provides sufficient buffer to avoid asurge in negative equity cases. (Source: HKET)   
    JPM View: During the 2016 Policy Address, HK Chief Executive CY Leung hasnoted that the government did not intend to relax the property market’s coolingmeasures as residential rents and home prices are still at unaffordable levels. Webelieve it is still too early to speculate on any possible withdrawal of the propertymeasures at the moment and the Government or HKMA will only start consideringany relaxation after another 10-15% decline. We think that as long as the stability ofthe banking system is maintained, the government is comfortable to see correction inthe residential market to continue gradually.

    We expect negative growth in 1Q16 given a strong base (y-o-y)   
    COSCO Pacific, a beneficiary of recent restructuring, remainsour top pick on potential special dividend   
    A weak start to 2016, despite front loading of shipments: Container throughput inthe top-eight Chinese ports declined 0.8% y-o-y in January 2016 vs. +0.9% y-o-y in4Q15. The slower throughput growth is despite some front loading of cargo this yearas the Chinese New Year holidays were earlier (starting 8 February) compared to2015 (19 February). We attribute the weak start in 2016 to a high base in 2015 (1Q15was up 7% y-o-y) and continued weak external demand. Indeed, Chinese exportsdeclined 11.2% y-o-y in January, the lowest reading since March 2015 (see China(Trade, January 2016) A disappointing start to 2016, 15 February 2016).   
    We expect negative growth in 1Q16 given a high base effect: We expect China’scontainer throughput growth to remain negative this quarter due to the weak externalenvironment and the high base of 1Q15 (+7.2% y-o-y). The China Purchasing ManagersIndex (PMI) for new export orders has been falling and has remained below 50 for morethan 12 months (see Caixin China Manufacturing PMI (January 2016) – A soft start to theyear, 1 February 2016). In January the new export orders fell at a faster pace, implyingrisks still appear to be on the downside in 1H16.We remain cautious on the growthoutlook for the rest of the year although we expect trade growth to rebound in Asia-Europe from disappointing growth in 2015 and stability in EUR vs. USD.   
    COSCO Pacific (Buy) remains our top pick with a TP of HKD10.60, given its attractivedividend yield and valuation and a stronger parent (post restructuring) is a plus (seerecent report Four Cs: consolidation, China, currency, and consensus, 2 February2016).We have a Buy rating on CMHI and a TP of HKD24.0 (trading at a five-yeartrough valuation following a sharp decline in its share price). What caught our immediate attention was that the bank’scapital has not improved HoH despite the issuance of USD650m AT1 bonds inNov-15. In our previous publication we expected BEA T1 and Total CAR ratiosto reach ~14.4% and 18.2% by Dec-15 implying ~60bp HoH improvement forboth. However, the reported numbers in fact came 10bp and 40bp lower HoH.   
    This was particularly surprising if we consider the following: total assets andloans were down ~4% HoH, and the pace of NPL growth in 2H15 at 19bp waslower than in 1H15. So where did the new capital go.   
    We noted the following trends that effectively negated the otherwise positiveimpact of the recent AT1 capital issuance: (1) BEA decided to increase thecoverage of its NPLs with provisions, which grew to ~60% from ~51% HoH;(2) this resulted in LLP/Pre-provision income doubling to 37% from 18.7% in2H15; and, most importantly, (3) the credit portion of BEA’s total RWA rose by10% in 2H15 leading to ~8% growth in total RWA, which is very contrasting tothe overall trend of shrinking loan book.   
    On the results briefing, the bank guided for its credit costs to remain elevatedin the near term given the weakening asset quality trend and subdued netinterest income generation in China, which attracted quite negativecommentary from the equity investors’ community. On a flip-side, the pictureis not so negative, in our view, from a credit stand point. The proactive creditrisk and capital management by the bank reaffirms its commitment toconservative recognition of credit risks and reduction of loans to the weakesttype of its borrowers. Thus, in 2015 BEA lowered its loan exposure to mosttrouble-making segments (hotels, retail trade and manufacturing) by ~35%.   
    We are not discouraged by the seemingly low level of LLR cover of NPLs of~60% given that (i) the bank is committed to increasing it, and (ii) over half ofimpaired loans get recovered. Moreover, 99% of BEA’s NPLs in China is fullycollateralised, including which the total LLR/NPLs would rise to ~130%.   
    Of course it is premature to talk about stabilising asset quality in China overall,however it is encouraging to see that in BEA’s case Chinese NPLs haveactually declined to 2.63% as of Dec-15 vs. 2.65% as of 1H15. BEA hasrecovered about HKD1.2bn and sold a moderate ~15% of Chinese NPLs in2H15, which helps the bank maintain the total NPL ratio under 1%. BEA hasalso confirmed that CaixaBank remains its long-term strategic shareholderdespite the recent reports (multiple sources including BusinessWire, 4-Feb) onCaixa “looking for an exit”. In our view, BEA remains amongst the bestcapitalised banks in EM.   
    Last week had brought a dramatic price correction to the global market of AT1bank bonds. BNKEA 5.5% Perps’c20 remain the most attractive paper in Asia,in our view, and are trading ~8 points lower vs. early Dec-15. We reiterate ourBuy recommendation on BNKEA 5.5% Perps’c20 (at current 92.5 askprice/7.4% ask-yield). We also affirm our Buy call on BNKEA 4.25% B3T224c19 bonds (at 98.68 ask-price/4.6% ask-yield) as they have visiblyunderperformed HK and Chinese peers since mid-Oct and yield-wise havefully converged with 10Y bullet B3T2 bonds of BCHINA (used to trade ~60bptighter just over six months ago).

<Ignored> SINA	EM Strategy &Economics-Colombia;:Fiscal Challenges Loom	摩根士丹利亚洲有限公司	摩根士丹利亚洲研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3126748/index.phtml	Colombia faces triple headwinds from a wider current accountdeficit, higher inflation, and a fiscal deficit due to lower oil prices forlonger. While the COP has further to weaken and we shift to MWfrom OW in local rates, we think much of the negative news is pricedin credit.   
    Economics: As Colombia’s economy adjusts to lower oil prices, three majorchallenges have emerged: a widening current account deficit, rising andpersistent inflation, and a deterioration of the fiscal accounts. We think thepolicy response to the three challenges should be twofold: further interestrates hikes would likely help curb inflation and improve the current account,while cutting government spending may be the only way to reach theauthorities’ fiscal objectives. In short, something’s got to give to rebalanceColombia’s economy and we suspect that economic growth is the weakest link.   
    Sovereign Credit: Given the recent spread widening, we think much of thenegative news is priced in sovereign credit, including the potential for slightlyhigher issuance and a move to a negative outlook by the rating agencies. Asustained rally in sovereign spreads would need oil prices to rebound.   
    However, we do favour Colombia to the other double-deficit credits, includingSouth Africa and Turkey, where problems are more structural. We therefore recommend buying Colombia 2044 vs. South Africa 2044 where investorscan also take advantage of the Colombian 10s30s curve being 70bp steeper.   
    Local Rates: We reduce our stance on Colombia's local rates from OW to MWfor three main reasons: (1) Macro risks have increased and we see a risk thecurve could re-steepen, especially given additional supply risks; (2) We expectinflation expectations will continue to rise and see the risk for monetary policytightening skewed toward the upside with respect to what is priced into thecurve; and (3) Colombia’s bonds no longer look as attractive on an expectedFX-hedged return basis, especially when compared to Mexico. We would henceshift exposure from Colombia to Mexico.   
    FX: We retain our bearish stance on COP and see USD/COP peaking at 3600 inthe third quarter. Oil prices remain the dominant driver of COP in the nearterm, but even if oil prices were to stabilize around our base case of $30, thiswill still place fiscal and external strains on the country. A weaker currency canhelp with these adjustments and is necessary to counterbalance the impact ofhigh inflation on the real effective exchange rate.

On the recentearnings call (see our take here), management noted that ~4,600 customers havesigned up for webinars, representing the largest ever registration for a newproduct. Customer feedback also indicates only slight overlap with MiSeq andas a result, ILMN expects minimal cannibalization (20-25%), with customerswho choose MiniSeq over MiSeq likely to opt for multiple units to optimizethroughput and sample flexibility.     The FY15 results season for Chinese developers is starting soon (with KWGreporting on Feb 19). While we expect solid and stable earnings growth forstate-owned leaders like COLI and CR Land, we see relatively low earningsvisibility for most private developers due to 1) slow contracted sales growth(negative for some developers) in 2015; 2) continued margin pressure as therise in contracted ASPs still lags behind increases in land costs in recent years;and 3) RMB depreciation leading to FX losses for those that booked FX gainsdirectly into P&L; in the past (instead of reserve on balance sheet).     Weak 2015 contracted sales growth leading to weaker top lines in FY15/6 P&L;   
    In 2015, the 25 listed developers that we track achieved average contractedsales value growth of 16% YoY and contracted GFA growth of 15% YoY.   
    However, 11 of the 25 developers achieved relatively slow or negative YoYgrowth in full-year contracted sales: Country Garden (+9%), Sunac (+4%),Wanda (+2%), CCRE (+1%), Sino Ocean (+1%), Agile (flat), R&F; (flat), KWG(-1%), Shimao (-5%), Greentown (-9%), CC Land (-12%). Also, on our analysis,among the listed developers, the average YoY growth rate in contracted ASPwas only 2.3% (after we adjusted for the smaller developers having significantchanges in geographical mixes), well below the YoY growth in land prices inrecent years, highlighting continued downward pressure on gross margins.   
    RMB depreciation also presents potential for negative surprises in P&L;   
    COLI, CR Land, Vanke and COGO have exchange reserves to offset initial RMBdepreciation, hence their P&L; should take relatively smaller hits (at least in theinitial phase of depreciation). However, most other developers (the majoritybeing private developers) chose to book their unrealized FX gains in P&L; in thepast when RMB was appreciating and so do not have Exchange Reserve onthe balance sheet. With RMB depreciating, the FX translation losses willdirectly hit their P&L.; As a reference, developers with higher gearing and ahigher amount of non-RMB debt face a bigger hit to their P&L; when RMBdepreciates; on our analysis, these developers include Evergrande, Yuexiu,Sunac, Sino Ocean, CCRE, Agile, Greentown, Shimao and KWG.   
    More focus on supply-side reform means significant demand stimulus unlikely   
    While we expect more policy relaxation by the government on the propertymarket (e.g. potential tax incentives, in addition to market-expected interestrate and RRR cuts), we expect the government to focus more on supply-sidereform (like cutting land sales and controlling construction scale) to addresshousing inventory issues in lower-tier cities, meaning that significant demandsideproperty market stimulus is unlikely in the near term. We recommendstaying selective: Buy state-owned names with good earnings visibility andgrowth prospects via continued market share gains, such as COLI, CR Land,Poly A, China Jinmao, and CSCEC, and names with restructuring upside, suchas Joy City and Greentown. We maintain Sell on names with weak earningsvisibility, high leverage and continued margin pressure: Sunac, Shimao,Evergrande, Country Garden, Yanlord, Agile, and Gemdale. We base our TPson NAV discounts. Risks: unexpected economic, policy/political volatility.

JPY appreciation(against the US$) negatively impacts Japan tech performance which will likelycontinue in the near term. On the other hand, TWD and KRW weakness againstthe US$ may offset the shortfall in core operations to some extent whilemeaningful EM currency weakness eventually reduces purchasing power inconsumption-driven markets such as China. Hence, we remain cautious onnames which have higher exposure to China.   
    Top picks and avoids: Most tech names are now trading close to their fwd bookvalue, but given a lack of visibility for earnings and lackluster end-demandoutlook, valuations will likely stay depressed until we see signs of demandimprovement (in 2H16 at the earliest). Meanwhile, we recommend investors staywith quality names such as TSMC and SEC, M/S gainers (Sunny Optical,Pegatron, Catcher) and high dividend plays (refer to Table 4 on page 5), whilewe remain cautious on companies with high exposure to EM (especially, China),second-tier brands, and M/S losers (LGE, HTC, Acer, etc.).

    The outperformance of Asian equities since the start of the US earnings season on21 January suggests that the market considers the threat to growth is now greater inthe developed world than in Asia. In the US, the issue is the possibility of weakerearnings growth and rising interest rates (not dissimilar to what happened in 1937).   
    Still, in China, the market continues to perceive the slow policy response to weakergrowth a risk.   
    Thus, while valuations are low, to see any sustainable recovery in Asian equities wewould need to see the following three factors playing out:   
    1. A change in Chinese policy to more proactively avert the threat of a growthslowdown   
    2. The Fed changing its thinking on the trajectory of US rates   
    3. Earnings growth simply holds up, either in the US or in Asia. But earningsseason in Asia so far gives little confidence that this is taking placeMeanwhile, since Q3 2015, Asian equity market correlations have started to shift.   
    This coincides with the Chinese currency embarking on a more volatile trajectory.   
    More recently, correlations of MSCI country indices to MSCI Asia ex Japan havefallen, in particular for Indonesia, Taiwan, the Philippines, Thailand and India. Here,local factors have started to play an increasingly important role in setting the pace forlocal equities.   
    The market turmoil also offers excellent opportunities to build access to what we call“Asia’s Best in Class” at reasonable valuations. These are companies with qualitiessetting them apart from the crowd in terms of management, innovative products,brand power or some other competitive advantage.

In considering the significance of the sell-off, we address three relatedquestions.

Global growth did slow last quarter, particularlymanufacturing output, which recorded declines in both November andDecember (see the research note “Global IP in search of footing” in thisGDW). However, part of this slowdown owes to temporary drags from unseasonableweather on DM household spending, inventory adjustments, anda continued intense pullback in commodity-producing sectors. We expectthese drags to fade as we move through the first half of the year, producinga modest rebound in manufacturing and GDP growth. While it is still earlyin the quarter, and Lunar New Year noise will cloud our ability to track activityin Asia, we note that the available data are consistent with this view.   
    Manufacturing projections for January are looking solid, labor market dataremain robust, and US retail sales beat expectations (Figure 1).   
    Are markets signaling a material tightening in DM credit conditions?Not yet. We expected EM credit conditions would tighten this year but hadanticipated that the DM credit cycle would be a tailwind for global growth.   
    To be sure, borrowing costs are rising and wealth effects are turning negative.   
    However, these drags should prove modest—and be offset to some degreeby falling oil prices—if they are not accompanied by funding marketstress and significant shifts in bank behavior. <Ignored> SINA	China Economic Watch:Upside su...	美林证券	美林证券研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3126693/index.phtml	A particularly strong set of money and credit data in January   
    Despite continued capital outflow, China money and credit data surprised on the upsidein January. New RMB bank loans rose to RMB2,510bn in January from RMB598bn inDecember (vs. market expectation of RMB1,900bn) and new total social financingincreased to RMB3,420bn from RMB1,820bn (vs. market expectation of RMB2,200bn).   
    The yoy growth of M2 growth accelerated to 14.0% yoy from 13.3% in December (vs.   
    market expectation of 13.5%), and that of outstanding loans and TSF also strengthenedto 15.3% and 13.3% respectively in January from 14.3% and 12.4% in December.   
    We expect macro policies to remain supportive against countercyclical headwinds, butwe doubt if the significant jump in credit growth will continue beyond January.   
    Improving liquidity, debt on-shoring and seasonality   
    We think the set of strong money and credit data suggests: (1) Better liquidity conditionsand easing expectations. Average interbank rate lowered by 107bp in Jan 2016 from a yearago to 2.11% and banks' expectation of relatively stable and supportive liquidity conditionssupported them to lend; (2) Seasonality coupled with strong bank competition. Bankstypically compete for good loan projects and rush to lend in January, and during aneconomic downturn, competition can be more fierce; and (3) Debt on-shoring. Domesticcorporates are repaying FX liabilities quickly amidst CNY depreciation expectations andreplacing them with CNY loans/bonds. Note that total FX loans contracted by US$6.8bn inJan 2016 vs. a gain of US$30.6bn in Jan 2015.   
    FX and capital flow the near-term policy focus   
    We think a near-term policy focus for the PBoC is to regain control on its currency andprevent excessive speculation of CNY depreciation and capital flight risks. We maintainour view that the PBoC will likely opt for maintaining CNY/USD exchange rate stability inthe near term, instead of free-floating the currency or initiating a large one-offdevaluation, coupled with tighter capital control measures (see Depreciation to winPBoC more freedom, 15 January).   
    In the near term, we think the PBoC will flexibly use its various liquidity managementtools to keep domestic liquidity adequate despite its hesitation to cut RRR amidstcapital outflow concerns. We maintain our forecasts for two cuts in policy interest ratesthis year, although the timing of the first cut may be further delayed until macro datapoint to further deceleration in growth. This would also be consistent with thegovernment initiative to cut excess capacity in some industrial sectors.

    EUR/USD   
    基本分析:   
    欧盟将于周四至周五(2月18日至19日)在布鲁塞尔召开春季峰会,有关英国是否能够继续留在欧盟的协商是此次峰会的主要议题之一。对此,澳新银行表示,对英镑而言,本周欧盟峰会将是关键测试。以下是该行主要观点:   
    英国首相卡梅伦在实现改革目标方面取得成功是关键。若欧盟峰会取得利好进展,即反对英国退出欧盟,则英国有关退出欧盟与否的全民公投料于6月23日得到确认。   
    “英国退欧”将为英国经济带来极大不确定性,需制定和实施退出欧盟的实际策略,将利空英镑。   
    在本周欧盟峰会后,卡梅伦和各媒体将需更好呈现既定改革的优点,以令英镑在汇市受到提振。若卡梅伦的行动“成功”,那么可能意味着英国退出欧盟公投可能较早,而非较晚举行。   
    因此,卡梅伦需聚集积极力量,以维持英国的欧盟成员国身份。这可能有助于消除当前笼罩于英镑的市场不确定性程度,不过主要取决于公投结果。目前投资者们仍宜采取观望立场。

Speaking against a backdrop ofheightened financial market volatility, US Fed Chair Yellen sounded a relativelydovish tone in her annual Congressional testimony. While the Fed Chair highlightedthe continued improved in US labour market conditions, she acknowledged thatfinancial conditions in the US and abroad had become tighter, and that this couldpotentially put the FOMC's expectations for steady economic growth this year at risk(see Yellen Testimony, 10 February 2016).   
    Softer US dollar tempers external stability concerns. Diminishing marketexpectations of Fed rate hikes has resulted in a weaker US dollar. The more benign USdollar environment will likely reinforce the dovish bias of regional central banks. Concernsabout external stability have at times prompted Asian central banks to become cautiousabout cutting rates into a U.S. tightening cycle. But these risks are fading.   
    Asian exports collapse in January; China yet to show signs of bottoming outInstead, deteriorating growth and rising disinflationary pressures remain the overwhelmingconcern for Asian policymakers. Disappointing January data only strengthens the case foradditional monetary easing. Korea, Taiwan, and China all reported significant exportdeclines in January, despite the fact that Lunar New Year effects should have distortedthe latest trade data to the upside. This points to a significant deterioration in global tradeat the start of 2016. Slowing growth in the mainland economy is clearly taking its toll.Unfortunately, we see few signs that growth is bottoming out.   
    More monetary and fiscal easing in the pipeline. In light of growing downside risksto what is already a tempered growth outlook, we expect further rate cuts from manyof the region's central banks, including in China, Indonesia, India, Korea, Australia,New Zealand, and Japan, where the Bank of Japan introduced a negative interestrate policy in January (see overleaf for a discussion of BoJ liquidity and its impact onAsia). Fiscal policy will also have to play a bigger role, especially in China, whereauthorities need to come up with a convincing package that includes greater fiscalexpansion in order to shore up private sector confidence in growth and reform (seeChina Inside Out: Beijing's five policy options, 2 February 2016).

    Tingyi's management expects it to take one to two quarters for competitors tofollow with a price hike (on instant noodles, from October 2015); we believeUPC is preparing for a new noodle launch in March/April 2016. We also thinkUPC will launch new flavors of Haizhiyan and Xiaoming Classmate to keep themomentum going this year. We think UPC's stream of new mid-/high-endproducts will sustain continuous margin improvement; upgrading to Buy.   
    Tingyi noodle: volume down and promotional expenses up   
    We visited a packaged food distributor in Guangzhou before Chinese NewYear. His company recorded 4-5% yoy growth for Tingyi noodle sales in 2015,primarily due to the price increase. He has seen Tingyi increasing promotionalsupport since the October 2015 price hike, and he estimates c.4-5% volumedecline. We lower our NPAT forecast by 5-13%, and accordingly our DCFbasedTP by 12% to HKD11.4 (9.5% WACC and 2% TG).We have a Buy rating because Tingyi started to strengthen R&D; and packagingin early 2015, and we see the potential for improvement in product innovationand pricing discipline, and a transformation from being a producer to a brand.Downside risks include intensifying competition leading to price cuts and risingselling expenses, and input cost hikes.   
    UPC: new product launches to stimulate sales   
    We see destocking risks in 4Q15 and 1Q16, as UPC starts to prepare for newnoodle and beverage launches, and therefore we revise down our 2015-16ENPAT forecasts by 7% and 2%, respectively, keeping our 2017E forecastunchanged. Based on end-2016 RMB forecast (previously based on mid-2016RMB forecast), we trim our DCF-based TP from HKD7 to HKD6.6 (8.84%WACC and 2% TG).   
    While we don’t see any sign of recovery in China, UPC’s new noodles andbeverages from March/April 2016 could create a stimulus for consumers, andits uninterrupted stream of new mid-/high-end products will help to sustainmargin improvement, which is the major growth driver in our 2016-17Eforecast. The latest market correction opens up a good opportunity to buy intoa strong player in the noodle and beverage market. Therefore, we upgrade toBuy from Hold. Key downside risks: input cost hikes, food safety issues,intensified competition.   
    Is there a future for instant noodles in China?   
    China per capita consumption was only 33 servings a year in 2014, notparticularly high amongst Asian peers (e.g. 74 in Korea; 58 in Vietnam, 56 inIndonesia), and we therefore believe China is not at risk of breaking thethreshold level (above which consumption of instant noodles becomeshazardous), if there is one. If it is only about health consciousness, we don’tsee why consumers are paying a premium for Nongshim Shin Ramen (whichsaw China sales breaking a record-high in 2015). To seek growth, noodlemakers should reach out for new consumers, i.e. the mid- and high-endmarkets. Longer term, we see revenue from chilled and frozen pasta andramen accounting for 22% of Nissin Food’s instant noodle sales in Japan, andit could also be the Chinese instant noodle market’s future, i.e. we are only atthe beginning stage of product mix improvement.

    In the face of macro headwinds are emerging markets still a growthdriver? Our macro analyst teams are bearish around EM growth prospectsgiven that many countries are clustering near the trough of the business cycle.Monetary policy is also perceived as out of sync with underlying economicneeds of various EM geographies. In this environment, we see EM as a mildheadwind given offsetting supportive dynamics in relative healthcare spendingand demographics , but certain companies likely face more pressure thanothers. Evidence also suggests that device businesses in oil producinggeographies (Saudi Arabia, Russia, Venezuela, Brazil) face a more challengingenvironment than low oil price beneficiaries like India, Korea, and to a lesserextent, China.

SINA	零售行业:黄金周未现拐点,2016还看成长与主题	国金证券股份有限公司	赵海春	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3126836/index.phtml	事件   
    据商务部统计,2016年春节黄金周7天,全国零售和餐饮企业实现销售额约7540亿元,同比增速11.21%(略微高于2015年春节11%的增速)。(1)增速,考虑CPI因素,几乎与2015年春节同比增速持平,自2009年以来黄金周社销同比增速持续下滑的态势未见显著拐点;(2)分商品看,保持较高增速的仍是金银珠宝、数码产品等消费升级类商品;(3)出境游及跨境购、文化消费等仍是春节消费上升热点。   
    评论   
    传统零售底部徘徊,转型拐点有待时日:我们认为,对于A股零售仍依赖实体门店主业为核心增长支撑的企业,道阻且长,业绩亮点有待时日。(1)实体零售面临CPI低位徘徊、消费低迷、电商及跨境购分流影响的格局并无见显著改善,2016年春节社销总额同比增速11.21%较2015年的11%增速仅略微增长;(2)分商品看,保持较高增速的仍是金银珠宝、数码产品等消费升级类商品,湖北重点监测企业金银珠宝销售额同比增长22%,宁夏、辽宁、吉林、内蒙古通讯器材销售额同比分别增长41.9%、20.6%、10.7%和8.5%;(3)据阿里的“中国年货大数据报告”,全国超过12000个农村淘宝服务站参加了阿里年货节,消费比平时增长331%,平均每笔订单为262元,较2015年春节的单笔增幅达到117%。;但多数A股企业的电商网站并未有阿里这样的平台效应,且我们认为,经济下滑带来的进城务工人员返乡增多及春节在家乡时间的增长或许也是农村春节购物增长的因素。   
    出境游、文化消费仍是消费上升热点,主题相关零售值得关注:我们认为,从出境游及其带动的跨境购(对国外历史积淀品牌的追逐)、票房消费额的爆增等,文化消费会是比传统商品零售有更好增速的内容;所以,建议关注迪斯尼开园主题受益类个股:百联股份、豫园商城、新世界、老凤祥等。(1)据国家旅游局发布的“全国旅游团队服务管理系统”数据,2015年春节假期出境游人数(不含港澳地区)达到518.2万人次,同比增长约10%,2016春节出境游人数将持续增长,增速有望超过10%,总人数预计达到570万到600万。如果以人均旅游费用以及购物等花费1.5万元计算,预计中国游客春节出境花费有望达到900亿。(2)根据时光网的Mtime PRO显示2016年春节电影票房收入近30亿、而根据《中国电影报》显示2015年同期票房仅18.2亿元,文化内容的消费成为高增长热点。   
    实体零售增速承压、文化消费占比尚小,穿越低迷或看转型高成长:(1)我们认为,2016年依赖实体零售门店为增长支点的零售企业将面临较严峻挑战,而文化内容消费及主题相关所带来的零售业绩增长或需要较长时间去实现,最有持续吸引力的线路,应该具备高确定性的高成长性;(2)而此类企业中,我们最看好商贸零售企业跨界转型的类型干细胞产业链、以及细胞免疫相关的转型企业。(3)首选行业内转型干细胞产业链以及细胞免疫相关的跨界转型企业。1、首推:南京新百(干细胞产业链上游脐带血库、移动养老龙头、医院资源丰厚)、国际医学(干细胞领军企业-汉氏联合的第二大股东、医院稳健)、新华锦(合作者利百健拥有SVF基质血管组分干细胞群专利);2、关注:转型医疗途中的百大集团(精准肿瘤治疗中心、上游布局)、杭州解百(转型医疗健康,方向确定)。

    主要观点   
    金融机构主要是为实体经济服务,《意见》的下发是金融机构服务实体经济的一个重要纲领。   
    《意见》主要提出了六个方面:加强货币信贷政策支持,营造良好的货币金融环境;加大资本市场、保险市场对工业企业的支持力度;推动工业企业融资机制创新;促进工业企业兼并重组;支持工业企业加快“走出去”;加强风险防范和协调配合。   
    目前,中国经济处于“三期叠加”的新常态之下,供给侧改革是“十三五”我国改革的全新路径,主要是去产能、去库存、去杠杆、降成本、补短板五大任务。   
    工业是国民经济的主导力量,根据中国国家统计局发布数据显示,2015年全国规模以上工业企业实现利润总额63554亿元,同比下降2.3%,是多年来首次下降。我国工业正面临的产能过剩、效益低下等问题,企业处于融资难、融资成本高的困境。   
    《意见》的下发明确了金融机构需应该在各方面加大力度给予支持,从银行差别化信贷政策、加大企业直接融资比例,促进工业企业兼并重组以推动行业整合、推进资产证券化发等多项措施,从而帮助工业企业在新常态下积极稳妥化解产能过剩、工业的转型升级、降低企业成本、增加效益、防范化解金融风险。   
    投资建议   
    八部委联合下发《意见》加大金融机构对实体经支持力度的同时,将有利于行业自身的发展:鼓励保险资管机构产品创新,为战略性新兴产业、先进制造业等提供资金支持,有利于保险资金配置走向实体经济呈现多元化。从加大企业直接融资比例到扩大公司信用类债券发行规模,有利于券商投行业务。引导银行业金融机构完善信贷准入标准,禁止对“僵尸企业”提供贷款有助于降低银行的不良资产。我们认为金融机构与实体经济两者之间是相辅相成的发展,因此我们给予金融业未来十二个月“增持”评级。	0.989943317334	中国铝业 0.00203647599029 华夏银行 0.00156688858403 西南证券 0.00150130144873 国新能源 0.00146863197856 中新药业 0.00133894527939	增长 增持	下降	医药生物 0.352108955383 商业贸易 0.189393743873 建筑装饰 0.17386727035 纺织服装 0.0815851613879 通信 0.056961927563	20160218	18:46

<Ignored> SINA	Commodity Matters:Crude realit...	摩根士丹利亚洲有限公司	摩根士丹利亚洲研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3126802/index.phtml	The launch of dozens of trade cases against Chinese crude steelexports has prompted questions over the sustainability of China'ssteel production rate. We find these cases are unlikely to significantlyalter China's exports in 2016.   
    China's steel sector's crisis of confidence: When the chapter on China'sindustrial rise is written in future history books, it may be that 2013 will bepinned as the peak. The potent combination of a large decline in fixed assetinvestment and construction activity halted the multi-year rise in China's steelconsumption at around 760 million tonnes (Mt). However, while in the twoyears since consumption has dropped to around 695Mt, actual steelproduction has not declined to the same degree. Steel mills were simply not ina position to cut production capacity, largely because of prohibitive debtburdens with local banks as well as social responsibilities to maintain localemployment, provincial GDP and fiscal revenue.   
    Exports up nearly twofold in two years: Consequently, steel mills andtraders turned to the export market as a release for excess capacity. With lowproduction costs versus global pears, China's steel products provedcompetitive across the world. After exporting 62Mt in 2013, the total reached112Mt by the end of 2015. Exports in January 2016 were 9.7Mt versus themonthly average in 2015 of 9.4Mt (see China Materials: January trade data:Iron ore and Copper Imports rebound continues , 15 Feb 2016).   
    Local steel producers arc up: Those cheaper imports have hurt recipientcountries' steel industries and unsurprisingly, many have launched trade casesagainst China. Nineteen countries responsible for 58% of China's exports(~65Mt) have either applied anti-dumping, anti-subsidy and safeguardmeasures, or launched cases gainst China. We counted at least 52 cases in2015 in which China-origin steel was named.   
    Total volume affected less than meets the eye: The potential effect of thetrade cases, coupled with the central government's focus on supply sidereform (see China Supply Side Reforms: Turnaround in Steel Outlook , 16Jan 2016) has prompted questions over the sustainability of China's steelexports and the knock-on effect to total steel production and demand for rawmaterials. However, we find that the total volume of steel trade affected bythese cases is much smaller than headline figures. According to our estimatesthat use CY2015's exports as a guide, just 15Mt of China's crude steel exportsare at risk in 2016, a figure that equates to 13% of 2015 total crude steelexports.

    Axiata 2020 sukuks (G+190bp, mid) are around 20bps wider YTD, slightlyoutperforming the broader Asia IG market that is 25-30bp wider (Figure 1). Wemaintain Hold. Key upside risks include tower sales in Indonesia and an IPO ofedotco. Downside risks are further supply from Axiata, inorganic growthstrategy and possible outflows for spectrum in Malaysia. Please refer to ourinitiation report on Jan 14 for more detailed credit views. Bharti 2023s(G+295bp offer) remain our top pick in the regional telco space.   
    Spectrum reallocation in Malaysia and payment of related fees - negative   
    Celcom’s spectrum holdings will be lowered from 2x17MHz to 2x10MHz in900MHz band and from 2x25MHz to 2x20MHz in 1800MHz band. Thespectrum would be fixed for a period of 15 years and the fees are yet to bedecided. The company has estimated additional capex for loss of spectrum atMYR1-2 billion over the next 10 years, which appears to be manageable.However, this does not take into account payment of the above mentionedspectrum fee or any possible acquisition by Celcom of spectrum in other bandsthat the government intends to release.   
    Deal with Telekom Malaysia (TM) - positive   
    This is an infrastructure sharing agreement which would allow Celcom accessto TM’s fiber backhaul infrastructure to accelerate its 4G rollout acrossMalaysia and to access the fixed broadband market. This should lower capexfor Celcom’s fiber requirements, though hard to quantify at this stage.   
    Bangladesh merger (and possibly Sri Lanka) - positive   
    Bangladesh will be a pure share swap and Axiata would hold 68.7% stake inthe merged entity. From a credit perspective, this is positive as it should lead tostronger revenue growth from wider network coverage and enhancedspectrum portfolio. Management estimates the merger will increase EBITDA by18-20% over the next few years. The merged entity will absorb ~USD90 millionof Airtel’s debt which increases Robi’s net leverage (3Q15 annualized) from0.5x to 0.8x (assuming no change in EBITDA) - Figure 2. Additionally, themerger should leave them with over 3000 excess towers that can possibly besold in the future or transferred to edotco. The transaction is expected to closein 2Q16. Separately, news reports suggest a possible acquisition of Airtel’s SriLankan operations by Axiata, valued at ~USD100 million (economynext.com) -we do not know if this will be via share swap or cash.   
    XL Axiata rights issue & tower sale- positive   
    XL Axiata is planning a rights issue to repay its USD500 million shareholderloan from Axiata Group. This should result in a net inflow to Axiata holdco aftersubscribing to its share (66.4%) of the rights issue. Company's eventual goal isstill to reduce the stake below 60% because of tax benefits if free float is morethan 40%. Additionally, XL is looking to sell up to 2,500 towers (Bloomberg).

<Ignored> SINA	Thailand household debt:Still feeling the weight	香港上海汇丰银行有限公司	香港上海汇丰研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3126776/index.phtml	Most of the talk in Thailand these days is about politics. A new draft constitution is tobe put to a referendum on 31 July 2016 and uncertainty about the outcome andsubsequent elections preoccupy most commentators. Less visible is the country’shigh household leverage, which will likely remain cumbersome at least through 2017.   
    Debt has expanded less rapidly over the past two years, but sluggish economic andwage growth, as well as diminishing farm incomes, have delayed the deleveragingprocess. We estimate that the household debt-to-GDP ratio will peak at around83.5% in Q4 2016. This means private consumption will likely remain weak andwhat will be needed is more public investment, especially on infrastructureprojects, to boost the economy.   
    We look closely at latest available, more detailed household data in the NationalStatistical Office’s household socio-economic survey for H1 2015, which we believeis unlikely to have changed materially over the past year. Things have gotten worsesince 2013 and households in rural areas, especially those in farming, remain mostvulnerable to negative shocks in the economy. Past government measures hadfocused on providing liquidity to the agriculture sector (e.g. cheap loans), but moreeffort could be put into existing measures, such as lowering production costs andraising farm prices. Meanwhile, non-farm professionals and city dwellers have higherincome and, therefore, more flexibility in dealing with debt, which helps explain theimprovement of some of the indicators of their indebtedness from 2013 to 2015.   
    Meanwhile, financial stability risks remain limited, given high capital adequacy ratios,even if non-performing loans (NPLs) have risen. The planned strengthening insupervision of non-bank lenders (e.g. state banks) will also help improve riskmanagement. Nevertheless, there are still downside risks to household debtsustainability from deflationary pressures. Last, but not least, we think that fiscalpolicy responses to future downside risks to growth should not be aimed atboosting consumption per se because that risks exacerbating the debtsituation. Instead, more targeted measures are needed. On the monetary front,the Bank of Thailand (BoT) is most likely to keep its policy rate on hold at 1.5%for an extended period.

SINA	亚厦股份:家装领域率先应用虚拟现实技术(VR)	东北证券股份有限公司	王小勇	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3127436/index.phtml	报告摘要:   
    虚拟现实(VR)技术和相关产业链逐步成熟,2016年或将全面爆发。虚拟现实(VR)是指通过计算机技术模拟创建的、可交互的三维虚拟世界,并通过接口设备给用户提供沉浸感觉的技术。2015年VR技术开始逐步崭露头角,索尼、三星等国外电子巨头旗下的VR产品逐步进入量产阶段,国内也有越来越多的企业开始进军VR领域,VR技术普及应用的条件逐步成熟,2016年或将全面爆发。   
    首创“VR+装饰”业务模式,打造2.0版视觉化客户体验,实现“蘑菇+”互联网家装平台的模式升级。“蘑菇+”是公司去年4月份推出的互联网家装平台,“蘑菇+”团队很早就开始了VR技术与平台装饰业务结合的研发。2月16日,公司表示“蘑菇+”的VR技术会随其家装业务开展一起推出,将主要用于销售端的虚拟样板房展示,以增强客户的体验感,预计今年3月份左右将会正式推出。届时,公司有望成为行业内第一家引入VR技术应用的装饰公司,借助VR技术为客户提供视觉化体验,实现“蘑菇+”互联网家装平台的模式升级。

SINA	钢铁行业财政注资投资基金“指导意见”点评:着眼经济结构调整	长江证券股份有限公司	王鹤涛	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3127426/index.phtml	以供给侧改革为主,适当扩大总需求:本次出台的“指导意见”更多指向战略性新兴产业等,但对于钢铁行业而言,仍有几点值得关注:1)意见指导思想落脚于“提高资源配置效率和财政资金使用效益,加快经济结构调整和发展方式转变”,表明其以经济结构调整为重点的根本动机;2)意见总体要求继续强调“市场在资源配置中起决定性作用,更好发挥政府引导作用”,由此表明坚持以市场无形之手主导经济发展仍是目前政策主基调;3)意见在重点支持产业中提到,“限定于具有一定竞争性、存在市场失灵、外溢性明显的关键领域和薄弱环节”,“对市场能够充分发挥作用的领域,要及时退出”,虽然不排除部分具有竞争性基建投资领域也含在内,但我们倾向于认为财政资金在投入领域上有选择性而非面面俱到应是此次意见所表达的重要思想。   
    总体而言,1月信贷等金融数据表现较好,使得市场对于总需求因此好转预期提升,而此次“指导意见”虽然只是财政资金运用规范的一部分,也并没有排除基建刺激的可能性,但却体现了坚持市场主导、坚持结构调整的政策倾向,预计未来一段时间相关政策的总基调大概率仍定位于“以供给侧改革为主,适当扩大总需求”。基于此,我们认为钢铁行业总需求短期相对稳定预期仍在,但超预期恢复可能性则大概率降低。   
    基本面与政策面配合,板块谨慎乐观:在目前两会前期改革政策面余温尚存,需求适当稳增长预期渐起,行业基本面在低库存、低供给环境下稳中趋强,叠加前期板块调整已释放部分风险的阶段,继续建议对于钢铁板块保持谨慎乐观态度,适当关注低估值质优标的首钢股份、宝钢股份、鞍钢股份、武钢股份、河钢股份、新钢股份、大冶特钢、华菱钢铁、方大特钢。同时,具有业绩等安全边际的转型、主题标的仍值得关注,包括国改预期强烈的韶钢松山、凌钢股份,转型预期法尔胜,受益于海外油气拓展顺利的玉龙股份,主业高增且具3D打印概念的中钢国际,打造供应链综合服务商的欧浦智网。	0.934299332322	国元证券 0.00155343427815 动力源 0.00132315188767 宝钢股份 0.00120618881194 国海证券 0.00097860516418 高新兴 0.000949098912912	增长	没有	建筑装饰 0.763849854469 非银金融 0.145577773452 传媒 0.0182560682297 化工 0.0132059687749 钢铁 0.0103364344686	20160218	21:26

<Ignored> SINA	Technology in Autos Speaker Series -1	摩根大通证券(亚太)有限公司	摩根大通(亚太)研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3127393/index.phtml	In Part 1 of our Tech-in-Autos Speaker Series, we hosted Christian Koehler, a partner at Strategy Engineers (specializedconsultants in the automotive industry), right before CNY. We present below key takeaways from the presentation:   
    Connected/Smart cars seeing a lot more activity globally, while EV has cooled down, except in China:Connected cars and Smart cars appear to have captured a lot more attention globally in the last 12 months with a lotmore developmental activity in Europe and Asia. On the contrary, the collapse in Oil prices has led to some cool-off inEV related activity in many markets. However, China remains an exception, given heavy government support.   
    Connected/Smart cars additive to components, while EV is likely to be reductive: Strategy engineers believeConnected/Smart cars are likely to be a bigger opportunity for components, since these would add more $$ content tothe automotive Bill of materials. On the other hand, EV is likely to simplify the existing power train and do away with alot of complicated components (ICE engine and related stuff) and replace that with a simple electric motor. Battery islikely to be the only big additional component, but that could become more commoditized as EV proliferates and morevalue moves to battery management systems.   
    Autonomous driving technology almost there, but the last 2% is likely to be expensive: Existing technologies canalready enable cars to make correct driving decisions in 97-98% of scenarios and perform conditional automation(traffic jam assist and highway driving, or so-called Level 3 of automation). Yet, full automation with 100% accuracy(Level 5 automated driving) requires a lot more intelligent functional software with machine learning-algorithms andhigher processing speed. This will take at least 2-3 more years to develop and is more likely to happen beyond 2020. Tofurther ensure safety, Strategy Engineers expect these functions to be firstly restricted in scenarios with 1) limiteddriving speed to minimize severity of potential accidents or 2) reduced complexity with no mixed traffic or pedestriansby 2020; whereas full function would be made available by 2025-30.   
    15% CAGR in connected car content growth until 2025 to $163bn, sensors and software key: Strategy Engineersexpect a strong 15% CAGR in connected car applications growth until 2025, with car-to-surroundings, car-toinfrastructure being the largest growth drivers. Consumer acceptance of assisted driving technology is highest in China,while technology advances remain fastest in the US and Germany. Functional software (that can enable fully assisteddriving functions) and sensors are likely to be the fastest growing components to enable a connected / smart car. Sensorscontent could grow 4x and account for up to 20% of new $ content in a fully autonomous car, while functional softwareand control units could both account for up to 10-11% of new content required in a full autonomous car.   
    Key disruptors for status quo – shared mobility, OTA updates, evolution of a horizontal supply chain: Threeareas stand out as key disruptors that current OEMs should watch out for: (1) Shared mobility (for commercial usethrough fleet tracking etc., or consumer use cases like Uber) could increase fleet utilization substantially whileshortening the replacement life of a car. (2) Customers getting accustomed to Over the Air (OTA) updates for their car,like Tesla, would challenge the way electronics are organized in a car. Currently, most cars have a lot of distributedelectronic components with no central processing, which is a model that is not suitable for easy OTA upgrades infunctionality. The new breed of car makers that want to take advantage of OTA etc. are moving towards much moreprocessing power residing centrally, more akin to an electronic device like a smartphone, (3) Auto supply chain ishighly vertically integrated with a fair bit of regionalization as well. As new technologies in connected cars evolve,especially around autonomous driving, the supply chain may need to become much more global and horizontal instructure.

    2015年运营商数据显示:中国移动终端活跃用户数最高的前20名apps中,腾讯开发或其投资的占据9席(其中微信、QQ以月活5.3、5.1亿分列前两名)、阿里占据5席(其中手机淘宝、支付宝以1.8、1.5亿月活分列第3、6名)、百度或其投资的占据4席;除BAT外,独立apps排名在前20的仅有2席(分别为360手机卫士和PPTV)。   
    C端流量的全面聚集在2015年加剧了O2O行业的恐慌,近期新崛起的独角兽公司无不被BAT归于囊下。“嘀嘀打车”、“饿了吗”也因为背靠巨大流量入口快速占据了出行和餐饮两个几乎最高频的O2O领域,在颠覆传统行业的同时颠覆了相关领域的同类先行公司,而互联网赢家通吃的这张独角兽船票也变得更加稀缺,寻找BAT做不了的领域似乎成了互联网战场的唯一出口。   
    2016年,企业级(2B)市场和新硬件市场将是我们值得思考和研究的两个重要方向。   
    B端资源整合、C端客户服务,互联网停车启航   
    伴随O2O资本寒冬,2016年或将成为O2O行业大规模去产能之年;而逆向思考,这也或将加速细分行业更快结束混战、去伪存真,新的龙头公司更快崛起之年。其中,“互联网停车”由于其刚性需求、B端属性、重资产重运营属性等,或将迎来快速发展之年。   
    随着互联网的发展,面向C端的社交网络和面向商品的电子商务已日渐成熟,尤其是进入移动互联网时代,通过智能终端,C端以实现普遍联网,移动支付等基础环境日渐完备,互联网下沉实体产业的条件同样已经成熟。另外,停车难带来的“出行之痛”是城市的痼疾,通过互联网把分散的停车场联接起来,破除信息孤岛,实现有限停车资源的优化配置使解决之道。“互联网+停车”市场在共享经济、资本涌入、政策利好三大驱动力下,各种停车Apps涌现,据不完全统计目前全国停车Apps远超100个。   
    2.传统停车行业痛点多,互联网停车大有可为   
    我国传统停车行业现状   
    1)总量缺口大:车多位少,停车位缺口大,保守估计,我国停车位缺口超过5000万个。2)结构较分散:配建为主、公共为辅、路侧为补充。3)管理散乱:缺乏专业化、集中度低,散而乱,配建停车场以业主自营和专业物业管理公司兼营为主;公共停车场以专业停车管理公司承包经营为主;整个停车场管理行业极度分散,以北京为例,备案停车场6581个,而管理方超过3000家。4)智能化水平低:智能化水平低,人工收费为主,艾瑞咨询调研显示,“北上广深”智能停车场覆盖率仅为7%;我国停车场智能设备配备率还处于低水平(设备市场规模/行业收费规模=37/5000),且以出入口控制系统为主(占80%左右);总体看来,国内大多数停车场依然采用传统的刷卡、取票的出入口控制方式,缴费方式主要是人工。	0.969548045074	中国联通 0.00120385894561 安居宝 0.00109520138003 捷顺科技 0.000990850646878 数字政通 0.000875834821195 中国建筑 0.000859194199606	活跃 利好		电气设备 0.949267923832 非银金融 0.0124109536409 计算机 0.00627644313499 公用事业 0.00490283221006 化工 0.00403259135783	20160218	21:26

The Exchange Rate Commission announced the end of Mexico’s FX interventionprogram. Instead, Mexico opted for a discretionary FX intervention program.   
    First, Finance Minister Luis Videgaray announced fiscal belt tightening in the form of spending cuts worth MXN 132.3bn (0.7%of GDP). The bulk of the cuts (MXN 100bn or 76%) will be done at Pemex, Mexico’s state-owned petroleum company. The restwill be in the form of cuts to current spending (60%) and investment spending (40%).   
    Then, Banxico Governor Agustin Carstens delivered the surprise knockout punch by announcing an intra-meeting 50bp policyrate hike to 3.75%. The decision was unanimous. The statement says external factors, including oil prices, have beenweakening the MXN, thereby increasing the probability that inflation expectations surge in a manner inconsistent with the 3%inflation target.   
    The statement adds that in light of today’s measures by the federal government and by Pemex to strengthen their finances, theBanxico board decided to fortify Mexico’s economic fundamentals in line with its delegated responsibility.   
    The statement makes it clear that this is a one-off hike and does not represent the beginning of a tightening cycle. The boardstated it remains tuned in to any changes in the factors determining inflation and inflation expectations, especially the exchangerate and possible FX pass-through to inflation. It will also vigilantly maintain Mexico’s monetary position relative to the US.   
    The impact of fiscal spending cuts on GDP growth should be minimal. The scale of fiscal spending cuts with direct impact onGDP is relatively small. The rate hike impact on growth should also be small. As we have shown elsewhere, Mexico’s financialand monetary conditions had eased substantially due to a weaker MXN, offsetting the potential impact of higher policy rates.   
    We applaud Mexico’s determined and coordinated policy efforts to strengthen the country’s economic fundamentals . With thisaction, Banxico can maintain its policy tied to the US Fed. We thus expect Banxico to remain on hold for the rest of the year inline with our US economists’ Fed call and our strategy team’s FX view. However, Banxico might hike once or twice more in 2016should a significant rise in the USDMXN jeopardise the bank’s inflation target or Mexico’s financial stability.

SINA	安邦集团每日经济	北京安邦咨询公司	安邦集团研究所	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3127296/index.phtml	2015年中国经济增速“破7”,国内生产总值为676708亿元,同比增长6.9%。这是全国的整体经济数据。如果从各地经济来看,则出现明显的“苦乐不均”。全国31个省、市、自治区,有的经济在崛起,有的在衰落,有的仍然保持领先优势。 据21世纪宏观研究院对各地经济数据排名的比对,2015年全国有约13个地区的经济总量位次出现变动。其中,前十名中有一半地区位次改变。2015年经济总量前5个大省,经济增速均为8%或者以上。如广东、浙江2015年经济增速为8%,均高于2014年的增速。西藏和重庆2015年经济增速均为11%,排名全国第一,均比2014年加快。重庆2015年经济总量超过了黑龙江。陕西、贵州、江西也分别超过内蒙古、新疆、天津的经济总量。广西也超过了天津、江西的经济总量。四川省从2014年的全国第八经济大省,2015年一举超越河北和辽宁,成为第六经济大省。 值得注意的是那些经济滑落的省份。尤为突出的是东北三省的集体滑落。据该院的数据,2015年东北三省的名义经济增速分别为:黑龙江-0.29%、吉林3.41%和辽宁0.26%(注:三省官方同比增速分别为5.7%、6.5%、3.0%)。与之相近的名义GDP增长率分别为山西0.32%、新疆0.55%、甘肃-0.66%(注:三省官方同比增速分别为3.1%、8.8%、8.1%)。 要指出的是,上述机构统计的各省名义GDP增速与各省官方公布的GDP增速有不小的差距。考虑到各地过去高报经济增速(尤其是在2015年)的可能,我们估计相关机构计算的名义经济增速应该出入不大。更值得注意的是,从2015年各省经济的升降沉浮可以看到,国内区域经济正在出现明显的“板块化”的分化现象,它不同于过去的东中西部区域划分,而是呈现更为局部的区域发展特点。东北地区作为最大的区域板块在持续经济“沦陷”,延续了2014年的发展困境;而深陷“煤炭诅咒”、产业单一的山西,以及西部的新疆、甘肃,也呈现出糟糕的发展状况。西部的四川、重庆成为内陆发展亮点,中部地区部分省分也在向前追赶,东部沿海发达省份仍然是领先军团。 值得关注的是,在经济增速排名的背后,反映的是各地在产业发展、人力资源、政策环境、金融资源、市场化程度、政府服务、思想观念等多种要素复合作用的结果。令人担心的是,国内某些地区的各种要素(如东北、山西等地)已经形成了负面向下的螺旋,积极的要素在持续流失,负面因素在不断堆积,形成了逐渐固化的经济社会塌陷,东北地区、山西、甘肃、新疆等地都有这种风险。 令人担心的是,随着国内快速交通网络的逐步完善,以及中国的市场化程度加深,国内地区间的各种要素流动速度会加快,而且更加市场化,区域经济发展将呈现出越来越强的“马太效应”--强者越强,弱者越弱。而且弱者的优质要素会流向强者,进一步削弱落后地区的发展基础。安邦咨询(ANBOUND)研究团队在国内所做的广泛的田野调查也证实了这一点。我们判断,这种“要素分化-经济差异”所形成的反馈循环将会不断强化,造成区域差异逐步“固化”。这意味着,落后的地区与其他地区的差距越拉越大,很难翻身。 最终分析结论(Final Analysis Conclusion): 随着市场要素流动加快,国内各个区域之间的发展差异将会加大,它会反过来进一步强化落后地区的要素流失。国内区域发展差异将会逐步固化,并且从经济领域蔓延到社会领域。这种趋势值得决策层警惕,也是以全面建成小康社会为战略目标的“十三五”需要应对的一个关键挑战!(AHJ)   
    〖优选信息〗   
    【形势要点:今年“去杠杆”政策可能保持较大弹性】   
    去年底召开的中央经济工作会议确定,中国2016年的五个主要任务包括:去产能、去库存、去杠杆、降成本、补短板。不过,面对2016年中国复杂的经济形势,这五个主要任务的实际执行恐怕不能简单地“一刀切”。中国经济在2016年面临的形势,可谓阴云密布。中国2015全年GDP增速为6.9%,是1990年以来最低。据路透社援引消息人士称,决策者对经济增长前景并不确定,预计可能将把今年经济增长目标设定在6.5-7%的区间内,这是中国首次设定经济增长目标区间。判断中国经济政策的一个基本逻辑,就是必须紧跟形势变化。野村证券中国首席经济学家赵扬称,“经济遭遇逆风,相信政府将推出更多措施来实现今年的经济增长目标,而这一目标可能在6.5%-7%之间。随着全球经济疲软,各国央行都在加大刺激措施,中国央行不可能在此时收紧政策。”野村证券的看法是有道理的。事实上,在春节假期后首日的国务院常务会议上,国务院总理李克强就强调,全球经济、特别是各国股市急剧下跌,也给中国经济带来很大的挑战和新的不确定因素,不过,“中国经济仍有巨大的潜力,我们有这么高的储蓄率,这么大的回旋空间,一旦经济真的出现滑出合理区间的苗头,该出手时我们会果断出手!”就此来看,中国今年的去杠杆政策不太可能简单“一刀切”,而是要根据形势、根据不同产业的情况而定。在日常的跟踪研究时,安邦咨询(ANBOUND)研究团队注意到,从银行信贷投放来看,部分领域就出现了加杠杆现象。有城商行人士称,目前贷款主要投放地产类20%、生产性企业30%、政府性项目50%,其中政府性项目包括债务置换,约占整体10%。据透露,目前有政府类项目利用政府信用,一个项目多方融资的情况出现。很显然,在政府关注的重点领域中,不是在去杠杆,而是在加杠杆。对市场来说,市场机会也要跟着政府项目和政府投资而动。(AHJ)   
    【形势要点:应加强扶贫成效考核评估的客观性和权威性】   
    中共中央办公厅、国务院办公厅近日印发《省级党委和政府扶贫开发工作成效考核办法》,旨在促使中国中西部22个省(自治区、直辖市)党委和政府切实履职尽责,改进工作。考核结果将作为对省级党委、政府主要负责人和领导班子综合考核评价的重要依据。之所以选在这22个省份,是因为当前中国14个集中连片特殊困难地区、592个国家扶贫开发工作重点县、12.8万个贫困村全部集中在中西部地区,贫困人口超过500万的省份如贵州、云南、河南、广西、湖南、四川等,也无一例外属于中西部地区。考核办法指出,考核工作将围绕落实精准扶贫、精准脱贫基本方略,针对主要目标任务设置考核指标,注重考核工作成效;坚持客观公正、群众认可,规范考核方式和程序,充分发挥社会监督作用;坚持结果导向、奖罚分明,实行正向激励,落实责任追究。据悉,考核工作从2016年到2020年,每年开展一次,由国务院扶贫开发领导小组组织进行。每年年底开始实施,次年2月底前完成,按省级总结、第三方评估、数据汇总、综合评价和沟通反馈等步骤进行。考核办法明确了扶贫开发工作成效四大考核内容,包括减贫成效、精准识别、精准帮扶和扶贫资金。值得注意的是,考核指标的数据来源除了扶贫开发信息系统、全国农村贫困监测等“官方”数据外,还将适当引入第三方评估。由国务院扶贫开发领导小组委托有关科研机构和社会组织,采取专项调查、抽样调查和实地核查等方式,对相关考核指标进行评估,充分发挥社会监督作用,使各项脱贫数据更加可靠、更加公正。然而,扶贫开发工作是全国性的政治任务和民生工程,无论是党政机关还是社会组织都难以置身事外,也就难以找到既客观又相对独立的第三方。扶贫开发工作既然是政治任务和民生工程,考核对象包括党委、政府主要负责人和领导班子,由此可借鉴中纪委巡视制度,由中纪委牵头,组建由国务院扶贫开发领导小组成员、科研机构专家和社会组织代表为主要成员的评估小组(如有必要可邀请联合国开发计划署官员共同参与),分派到全国各地区进行评估考核。(LPL)   
    【形势要点:多因素导致1月国内土地市场骤然降温】   
    2016年1月份,土地市场延续2015年的分化现象。一方面,杭州、南京等热点二线城市高溢价地块频出,并且接连刷新城市单价地王纪录;另一方面,从整体来看,全国土地市场的成交规模却显著缩减,部分城市同比跌幅甚至超过50%。市场机构CRIC的监测数据显示,2016年1月份,全国300城市经营性土地成交金额910亿元,同比大跌23%;成交建筑面积2615万平方米,同比骤降45%,为近五年的1月份新低。分城市类型来看,一线城市成交量下跌最为明显,1月份土地出让面积同比下滑七成,同样为近5年以来最低。据CRIC整理,2015年一线城市计划出让经营性土地3417万平方米,但最终仅成交了2000万平方米。虽然国土部一再要求供不应求的城市加大土地供应,但受到拆迁成本高、建成区土地储备几近枯竭、公共设施承载力不足、土地流转受限等因素影响,一线城市的土地出让量仍难抬头。近期宣布降低土地出让总量的深圳市,更是个中典型。分析人士认为,1月土地市场整体降温,主要受到三方面影响:首先是行业周期,传统淡季导致环比大跌;其次是需求热度降温,经历了2015年下半年的高热之后,地价已达高位。且市场需求在2015年有效释放以后,后继乏力;除此以外,最重要的还是政策严控,1月份国土部再一次明确表态,2016年仍将聚焦去库存,对于住宅用地政策将“有保有压”。(RWX)   
    【形势要点:国家重点研发计划将“脱胎换骨”】   
    “973计划”“863计划”即将成为历史名词。国家重点研发计划首批重点研发专项指南已于2月16日发布,这标志着整合了多项科技计划的国家重点研发计划从即日起正式启动实施。为解决原有科技计划体系的重复、分散、封闭、低效等问题,进一步提高财政资金使用效益,国务院于2014年部署国家科技计划管理改革,计划在2016年底前完成改革主体任务,将原有的100多个科技计划整合成国家自然科学基金、国家科技重大专项、国家重点研发计划、技术创新引导专项(基金)、基地和人才专项五大类。其中,国家重点研发计划是改革的重中之重,也是五类计划中启动最早的一项改革。科技部副部长侯建国说,国家重点研发计划整合了原有的973计划、863计划、国家科技支撑计划、国际科技合作与交流专项,发展改革委、工信部管理的产业技术研究与开发资金,以及有关部门管理的公益性行业科研专项等内容。计划主要针对事关国计民生的农业、能源资源、生态环境、健康等领域中需要长期演进的重大社会公益性研究,以及事关产业核心竞争力、整体自主创新能力和国家安全的战略性、基础性、前瞻性重大科学问题、重大共性关键技术和产品、重大国际科技合作等。他表示,国家重点研发计划目前形成了59个重点专项的总体布局和优先启动36个重点专项的相关建议,经国家科改领导小组审议通过后,现已得到国务院批准。财政部教科文司副司长霍步刚表示,正在进行的国家科技计划管理改革不是对原有科技计划的简单归并,计划整合完成后,财政科技投入将不会减少。截至目前,原有的100余项科技计划中已有将近90%完成整合。科技计划的整合不是“为整合而整合”,而是为了提高科技创新效率,聚焦国家重大战略需求,形成全链条、一体化设计。财政科技投入不会因为科技计划的优化整合而减少,相反,对高校和科研机构的稳定经费支持和基础研究的财政投入将进一步加大。(RLEQ)   
    【形势要点:美国对华制造业及服务业投资比重大幅增加】   
    商务部17日召开发布会,通报2016年1月份我国商务运行情况。最新统计数据显示,1月份美国对华投资增幅达到463.6%。针对美对华投资的大幅增长,沈丹阳表示,美国对华投资大幅增长原因主要有两个:一是去年同期基数较低。2016年1月,美国实际投资47.17亿元人民币,而2015年同期美国对华实际投资仅为8.37亿元人民币。二是与我国进一步扩大开放和一些美国企业继续看好中国市场有关。从增长的行业看,美国企业主要在制造业、交通运输、仓储邮政、信息软件、租赁和商务服务、科研等领域增加对华投资。(RLEQ)   
    【形势要点:中石油为自己叫屈的理由不能成立】   
    2月16日,中石油首次在微信公众号上发文《美国油价比中国便宜的内幕》,为油价贵做解释。中石油的文章里说了三点,第一就是美国油比中国多,截至2014年底,美国石油探明储量为48.5,中国为18.5(单位:十亿桶)。不容忽略的是,美国人口不到中国的四分之一,一个“油多人少”,而另一个“油少人多”。第二说的就是税了,在美国,采用的是税价分离的计费方式,油价是油价,税是税,你掏一升油钱,还要额外再掏一份税金。并且,美国各州的税率不一,纽约州、北卡罗来纳州和加利福尼亚州的成品油税最高,分别是每加仑交42.4、40.7和39.5美分的税。而在中国,我们采用的是成品油实际消费价和税混合在一起的计费方式。按照我国的成品油价格结构,油价中的48%为各种税费。以5.67元/升的92号汽油为例,如果刨去税款的话,那么每升价格应为2.95元,与美国多数加油站的价格实际上是持平的。第三说中国的油其实不贵,相比于德国和韩国,中国的油价还是便宜的。德国成品油消费税为57%、韩国为52%。中石油说这些是想表达一点,那就是油贵是因为税收的太多,责任不在我。安邦咨询(ANBOUND)研究团队认为,中石油为自己叫屈的理由是不能成立的。首先,中美两国人均收入差别极大,按照绝对价格计算,我们的油价比美国不知要贵多少倍。这种能源负担,也是企业的成本居高不下的一个主要原因。其次,税收取之于民用之于民,外国高税收的目的就是抑制消费,引导消费。德国和韩国用这笔消费税来改善环境发展公共交通。但国内只收税的时候像国际高标准看齐,税收上来后就结束了,空气治理、环境改善,以往一样也没有真正去做。第三,中石油每年从国家获得了巨额补贴,这是世界少有的国企特权。一年上千亿的利润加上巨额补贴还哭穷,实在没道理。最后,美国之所以现在油价越来越便宜,是因为美国民间企业开采页岩油成功,大大改善了美国的能源结构,从石油进口国变成了石油出口国。而在国内,中石油在国内就是寡头垄断,扼杀了民营企业的市场空间和创新力,而中石油躺着都赚钱,自然也无心搞市场开发和创新。因此,中石油的辩解很难令人信服,也缺少诚意。(RZJX)	0.888630286224	中国石油 0.00889348631322 鄂尔多斯 0.00669749739289 中国铝业 0.00661300662071 动力源 0.00421522644098 新希望 0.003194555917	增长 优势 完成 获得	下跌 然而 难以 跌幅 大跌 下滑 减少 没有	采掘 0.487302601337 电气设备 0.281621307135 传媒 0.0464567244053 建筑装饰 0.037398211658 食品饮料 0.0337531454861	20160218	21:26
SINA	汽车行业:丰田收购大发剩余股权事件点评,丰田收购大发进军小微...	渤海证券股份有限公司	郑连声	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3127292/index.phtml	事件:据日媒报道,丰田汽车宣布将收购子公司大发汽车的所有股权,双方在小型车领域展开合作,实现技术共享并继续发展业务。   
    点评:   
    丰田重视开发小微型汽车领域   
    迫于全球市场节能减排的压力,丰田近几年正在提升对小型车的重视,以更好地开拓印度等新兴市场。比如在铃木遥遥领先的印度市场,丰田邀请大发帮助其开发廉价小型车,以更好地开拓当地市场。我们预计,未来丰田与大众的销量冠军之争,性价比高的小微型车领域将是重点。   
    一汽系或受益   
    落脚到国内,大发早前就跟夏利与一汽吉林有过合作,但都没有取得成功。而国内当下以上汽通用五菱为代表的小微型车销量可观,或许会在某种程度上引起丰田及大发对中国小微型车市场的再度重视。因此,未来不排除丰田借助大发在小微型车领域的技术优势以及丰田自身在国内的销售渠道优势,再度与合作伙伴夏利及一汽吉林合作开发小微型汽车的可能。这一方面可以解决丰田在小微型车领域的短板,巩固销量冠军优势;另一方面,也可以帮助夏利度过经营难关。   
    建议积极关注*ST夏利及一汽轿车的投资机会   
    不管今年一汽系能否完成整体上市,我们认为,提升一汽旗下整车及零部件资产的盈利能力是重点。目前来看,与合资伙伴大众、丰田加强合作可能是主要思路之一。因此,如果一汽与丰田、大众合作出现新进展,对一汽整体上市及以后的业绩增长都是好事,建议关注*st夏利与一汽轿车的投资机会。

SINA	证券行业:IPO发行节奏缓慢,有利于市场的进一步反弹	中国中投证券有限责任公司	张镭	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3127262/index.phtml	事件描述   
    2月16日,证监会布按法定程序核准了9家企业的首发申请。其中,上交所4家,深交所中小板2家,创业板3家。证监会要求上述企业及其承销商将分别与沪深交易所协商确定发行日程,并陆续刊登招股文件。   
    点评:   
    从节奏来看,较为缓慢。首先与2015年相比,2016年发行节奏放缓许多。2015年除去中间暂停的5个月,IPO月均数达到30家,而2016年以来共核发16家。其次与IPO审核通过数量相比,核准发行数量也偏少。1月份,通过IPO审核阶段的公司就有34家,目前通过审核但未发行的公司已累计109家。我们认为注册制实施之后,第一步将会安排消化这些排队公司,届时每月核发公司数有望超过30家。   
    监管层呵护市场之心坚决。在2016年1月8日证监会例行发布会上,新闻发言人邓舸表态“证监会将会根据市场和交易系统初期运行情况,按照有利于增强市场活力、维护市场稳定的原则,合理安排新股发行”。其中二级市场稳定是监管层主要观测指标。尽管节后开市迎来了三个阳线,但考虑到2016年1月份上证综指大跌了22.7%以及春节期间全球主要股市大幅下跌,监管层对IPO发行仍选择保守态度。   
    新股发行对市场的影响主要存在于心理层面。在旧规下新股发行需提前冻结资金,对股市有很强的抽血效应,但新股发行新规已取消预缴款制度,新股发行不会对资金面形成很大冲击。近几年上市公司并购重组火爆,企业增发发展迅猛,在募集资金规模方面已经大幅超过新股发行募集资金规模,2015年全年新股发行募集资金规模为1472亿元,而增发募集资金规模高达9947亿元。   
    投资要点:   
    IPO发行节奏缓慢,有利于市场的进一步反弹。猴年开市迎来了三根阳线,在此背景下,监管层对IPO发行仍较为保守,没有大规模放量,凸显监管层对市场呵护之心的坚决,有利于市场进一步反弹。   
    自营盘压力释放。券商1月份业绩环比下降9成之多,券商自营业务是罪魁祸首,市场的大跌对自营业务形成巨大压力。但我们应该看到1月份大部分券商仍维持正收益,其次自营盘压力已经释放,每一次反弹对业绩的影响都将是正面的。   
    前期超跌已具备一定安全边际。券商板块2016年以来下跌了24.6%,跑输大盘5.7个百分点。我们重点推荐华泰证券(601688)、广发证券(000776)。

    互联网+标准化+定制化,打造管家服务新标杆:公司通过自主研发的“园林管家”APP,实现在线服务、网上下单、订单管理、新品发布等功能,打造020信息化平台,通过互联网技术降低沟通成本。同时管家服务按照职业规范进行标准化,从服装到公司配送车辆图标细节都采用标准化管理,实现标准化服务。定制化增值服务,预留增值服务入口,未来提供高端设计圈子和业主圈子,为高端用户提供定制  化服务。

SINA	新能源专题(二):海上风电破冰进行时	国联证券股份有限公司	马宝德	http://vip.stock.finance.sina.com.cn/q/go.php/vReport_Show/kind/search/rptid/3127244/index.phtml	海上风电将成为风电进一步发展的新蓝海。海上具有更强更稳的风力资源,海上风机具有更大的单机容量以及更高的利用小时数,此外海上风电场紧邻负荷中心,无弃光限电的忧虑。因此海上将成为未来风电进一步发展的必然方向。我国具有约18000公里海岸线,海上风能资源技术开发量达500GW,发展潜力巨大。   
    欧洲领衔全球海上风电,我国蓄势待发。2014年全球海上风电累计容量达到了8759MW,相比2013年增长了24.3%。截至2014年底全球91%(8045MW)的海上风机安装于欧洲的海域,为全球海上风电发展的中心。我国同样具备发展海上风电的基础,目前标杆电价已到位,沿海省份已完成海上风电装机规划,随着行业技术的进步、产业链优化以及开发经验的累积,我国海上风电将逐步破冰,并在“十三五”期间迎来爆发,至2020年30GW的装机目标或将一举突破。   
    投资机会梳理:海上风电产业链包括海上风机的制造,运输和安装,海底电缆的制造及敷设以及海上风电场的运行和维护等环节。   
    风机制造环节,我们推荐风机龙头金风科技(002202.SZ),其直驱永磁技术更适用于海上风机,目前已有2.5MW、3.0MW和6.0MW系列化产品;海上安装船环节,我们推荐上海佳豪(300008.SZ),民营船舶龙头设计过“双体海上风电工程专用船”,以及自升式多功能辅助平台,具备海上风电安装船的研发、设计与制造能力;海底电缆环节,我们推荐中天科技(600522.SH),公司海缆产品最早进入国际市场,具有完整的军品供货资质,在技术研发、产品质量、供货业绩等方面处于领先地位。   
    海上风电场开发与运维环节,我们推荐龙源电力(0916.HK),公司是全球最大的风电开发商,也是国内的海上风电开发急先锋,公司2014年新投产海上风电装机容量达88兆瓦,累计容量344.3兆瓦,占全国在运行机组容量的52.3%,2015年又有136MW海上风电项目投产,2016年公司计划开工至少200MW,增速迅猛。   
    风险因素:(1)标杆电价过低的风险;(2)运维经验缺乏的风险;(3)开发进度不及预期的风险;	0.998447966516	国新能源 0.00110830143028 天顺风能 0.000943114827093 中海海盛 0.000891013921023 华锐风电 0.00088769480725 华电国际 0.000822209075267	增长 完成		公用事业 0.670006155968 采掘 0.300328880548 有色金属 0.0184623096138 机械设备 0.00448401877657 建筑材料 0.0019763216842	20160218	21:26
